         <h1 class="texto">
          <a class="cbArticle" data-metrics="mod-6;noticias" data-uol-see-later="url" href="https://noticias.uol.com.br/ultimas-noticias/ansa/2021/03/21/merkel-planeja-estender-lockdown-na-alemanha-ate-abril.htm" name="manchete-noticias-modulo1">

           <span class="chapeu cor2 cor2-p4 cor18-hover cor-transition">
            Combate à pandemia
           </span>
           <span class="linha font1 cor2-hover cor2-p4-hover cor-transition">

            <span class="comentariosContainer">

;var echo=(function(window,document,undefined){var store=[];var offset;var throttle;var poll;var _inView=function(el,i){try{var coords=el.getBoundingClientRect();var topScroll=(window.pageYOffset||document.scrollTop||0)-(document.clientTop||0);return el.offsetWidth>0&&((coords.top>=0&&coords.left>=0&&coords.top)<=(window.innerHeight||document.documentElement.clientHeight)+offset&&(topScroll+coords.top+offset>=topScroll));}catch(err){store.splice(i,1);}};var _pollImages=function(){for(var i=store.length;i--;){var self=store[i];if(_inView(self,i)){_loadImage(self);store.splice(i,1);}}};var _throttle=function(){clearTimeout(poll);poll=setTimeout(_pollImages,throttle);};var _storeImg=function(nodes){var t_images=nodes.length;for(var i=0;i<t_images;i++){var img=nodes[i];var className=img&&img.className?img.className.toString():"";if(className.match(/lazyload/)){if(img.getAttribute("data-original")||img.getAttribute("data-src")){store.push(img);}else{_removeImage(img);}}}};var _removeImage=function(image){image.parentNode.removeChild(image);};var _imageLoaded=function(event){var image=event.target;image.classList.add("loaded");};var _imageError=function(event){var
